Migration: Findings\\n\\nThis analysis identifies all Java source files in apache/kafka (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489) that implement the Kafka Streams DSL (map, filter, groupBy) operations and their corresponding Processor API equivalents, supporting migration from the high-level DSL to the lower-level Processor API for custom state store management.\\n\\n### Architecture Overview\\n\\nThe Kafka Streams codebase follows a clear separation between the DSL and Processor API layers:\\n\\n**Processor API Foundation** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/api/):\\n- `Processor.java`: Core interface for stream records with arbitrary key/value type transformations\\n- `FixedKeyProcessor.java`: Optimized processor for fixed-key streams (key doesn't change)\\n- `ProcessorSupplier.java`: Factory interface for creating Processor instances\\n- `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier.java`: Factory interface for creating FixedKeyProcessor instances\\n- `ContextualProcessor.java`: Base class extending Processor with processing context access\\n- `ContextualFixedKeyProcessor.java`: Base class extending FixedKeyProcessor with processing context access\\n- `Record.java` and `FixedKeyRecord.java`: Record wrapper interfaces\\n- `ProcessorContext.java` and `FixedKeyProcessorContext.java`: Context interfaces for state store access and record forwarding\\n\\n### Core DSL Operations\\n\\n**1. Map Operation**\\n- **DSL Entry Point**: `KStreamImpl.map()` (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamImpl.java:283-300)\\n- **Processor Implementation**: `KStreamMap.java` implements `ProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KOut, VOut>`\\n- **Inner Processor**: `KStreamMapProcessor extends ContextualProcessor<KIn, VIn, KOut, VOut>`\\n- **Key Pattern**: Transforms both key and value, changing key type (key-changing operation)\\n- **Record Flow**: `KeyValueMapper` applies transformation, `context().forward()` sends modified record\\n\\n**2. Filter Operation**\\n- **DSL Entry Point**: `KStreamImpl.filter()` (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamImpl.java:146-172)\\n- **Processor Implementation**: `KStreamFilter.java` implements `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<K, V, V>`\\n- **Inner Processor**: `KStreamFilterProcessor extends ContextualFixedKeyProcessor<K, V, V>`\\n- **Key Pattern**: Keeps fixed key, filters based on `Predicate<K, V>` test result\\n- **Record Flow**: Conditional forwarding using `context().forward(record)` only if predicate passes\\n\\n**3. MapValues Operation**\\n- **DSL Entry Point**: `KStreamImpl.mapValues()` (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamImpl.java:241-280)\\n- **Processor Implementation**: `KStreamMapValues.java` implements `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, VOut>`\\n- **Inner Processor**: `KStreamMapProcessor extends ContextualFixedKeyProcessor<KIn, VIn, VOut>`\\n- **Key Pattern**: Transforms value only, preserves key type\\n- **Record Flow**: `ValueMapperWithKey` transforms values, `context().forward()` sends modified record\\n\\n**4. GroupBy Operation**\\n- **DSL Entry Point**: `KStreamImpl.groupBy()` (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamImpl.java:693-716)\\n- **Repartitioning**: Creates a key-changing operation using `internalSelectKey()` which applies `KStreamMap`\\n- **Result**: Returns `KGroupedStreamImpl<KOut, V>` for downstream aggregations\\n- **GroupedStreamAggregateBuilder**: Orchestrates repartitioning and stateful aggregation processors\\n\\n### Extended DSL Operations\\n\\n**FlatMap/FlatMapValues**:\\n- `KStreamFlatMap.java`: Implements `ProcessorSupplier` for 1-to-many key-value transformations\\n- `KStreamFlatMapValues.java`: Implements `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier` for value-only expansions\\n\\n**Stateless Operations**:\\n- `KStreamPeek.java`: Implements `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier` for side-effects without modifying records\\n- `KStreamBranch.java`: Implements `ProcessorSupplier` for conditional routing to multiple child nodes\\n- `KStreamPrint.java`: Implements `ProcessorSupplier` for debugging/printing records\\n- `ForeachProcessor.java`: Implements `Processor` for terminal side-effect operations\\n\\n**Stateful Aggregation**:\\n- `KStreamReduce.java`: Implements `KStreamAggProcessorSupplier` for reduce operations with state stores\\n- `KStreamAggregate.java`: Implements `KStreamAggProcessorSupplier` for aggregate operations with initialization\\n- `KStreamWindowAggregate.java`: Time-windowed aggregation processor\\n- `KStreamSessionWindowAggregate.java`: Session-windowed aggregation processor\\n- `KStreamSlidingWindowAggregate.java`: Sliding window aggregation processor\\n\\n### KTable DSL Operations\\n\\n**KTable.filter()**:\\n- **Processor Implementation**: `KTableFilter.java` implements `KTableProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KIn, VIn>`\\n- **Inner Processor**: `KTableFilterProcessor implements Processor<KIn, Change<VIn>, KIn, Change<VIn>>`\\n- **State Management**: Materializes state store if queryable, tracks old/new values for changelog semantics\\n\\n**KTable.mapValues()**:\\n- **Processor Implementation**: `KTableMapValues.java` implements `KTableProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KIn, VOut>`\\n- **Inner Processor**: `KTableMapValuesProcessor implements Processor<KIn, Change<VIn>, KIn, Change<VOut>>`\\n- **Change Records**: Operates on `Change<V>` wrappers to track old and new values for updates\\n\\n**KTable Joins**:\\n- `KTableKTableAbstractJoin.java`: Base for table-table joins (inner, left, right, outer)\\n- `KTableKTableInnerJoin.java`, `KTableKTableLeftJoin.java`, `KTableKTableRightJoin.java`, `KTableKTableOuterJoin.java`\\n- `KTableKTableJoinMerger.java`: Merges results from multiple join sides\\n\\n**KStream-KTable Joins**:\\n- `KStreamKTableJoin.java`: Stream-table join processor\\n- `KStreamKStreamJoin.java` and variants: Stream-stream joins with windowing\\n\\n### Implementation Patterns\\n\\n**KStream Pattern** (Key or Value Changing):\\n1. Call DSL method on `KStreamImpl` (e.g., `filter()`, `map()`)\\n2. Create `ProcessorParameters` with a `ProcessorSupplier` instance (e.g., `new KStreamFilter(predicate, false)`)\\n3. Wrap in `ProcessorGraphNode` for topology building\\n4. Return new `KStreamImpl` with graph node reference\\n5. Inner processor class extends `ContextualProcessor` or `ContextualFixedKeyProcessor`\\n6. Process method calls `context().forward()` to send records downstream\\n\\n**KTable Pattern** (Stateful):\\n1. Call DSL method on `KTableImpl` (e.g., `filter()`, `mapValues()`)\\n2. Create processor supplier implementing `KTableProcessorSupplier`\\n3. Processor receives/sends `Change<V>` records (tracking old and new values)\\n4. Materializes state store for queryability and changelog management\\n5. Manages old value state for changelog semantics\\n\\n**Grouping Pattern**:\\n1. `KStreamImpl.groupBy()` creates key selection using `internalSelectKey()` \\n2. Returns `KGroupedStreamImpl` which chains to aggregation builders\\n3. `GroupedStreamAggregateBuilder` orchestrates repartitioning and aggregation processor deployment\\n4. Aggregation processors use state stores for incremental computations\\n\\n### Migration Implications\\n\\nFor teams migrating from DSL to Processor API for custom state store management:\\n\\n1. **Direct Replacement**: Single-operation transformations (map, filter, mapValues) can be replaced with corresponding `Processor` implementations\\n\\n2. **State Store Access**: KTable and aggregation operations require understanding of `Change<V>` records and state store lifecycle (`init()`, `close()` methods)\\n\\n3. **Record Forwarding**: DSL `context().forward()` calls must be preserved in custom processors for proper topology connectivity\\n\\n4. **Processor Suppliers**: Must implement appropriate supplier interfaces (`ProcessorSupplier`, `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier`, `KTableProcessorSupplier`)\\n\\n5. **State Management**: Stateful operations require explicit `StoreBuilder` configuration and `StoreFactory` integration\\n\\nThe clear separation between `FixedKeyProcessor` (for same-key transformations) and `Processor` (for key-changing transformations) enables compiler-level safety and performance optimizations by avoiding unnecessary key serialization overhead.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":8,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1138,"cache_read_input_tokens":94467,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1138},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"a6cc2c77-c3c3-4e65-9fed-56d35a54acba","uuid":"42dd562d-6912-4ff7-91ae-8c4348e3c66e"}

Migration: Findings\\n\\nThis analysis identifies all Java source files in apache/kafka (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489) that implement the Kafka Streams DSL (map, filter, groupBy) operations and their corresponding Processor API equivalents, supporting migration from the high-level DSL to the lower-level Processor API for custom state store management.\\n\\n### Architecture Overview\\n\\nThe Kafka Streams codebase follows a clear separation between the DSL and Processor API layers:\\n\\n**Processor API Foundation** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/api/):\\n- `Processor.java`: Core interface for stream records with arbitrary key/value type transformations\\n- `FixedKeyProcessor.java`: Optimized processor for fixed-key streams (key doesn't change)\\n- `ProcessorSupplier.java`: Factory interface for creating Processor instances\\n- `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier.java`: Factory interface for creating FixedKeyProcessor instances\\n- `ContextualProcessor.java`: Base class extending Processor with processing context access\\n- `ContextualFixedKeyProcessor.java`: Base class extending FixedKeyProcessor with processing context access\\n- `Record.java` and `FixedKeyRecord.java`: Record wrapper interfaces\\n- `ProcessorContext.java` and `FixedKeyProcessorContext.java`: Context interfaces for state store access and record forwarding\\n\\n### Core DSL Operations\\n\\n**1. Map Operation**\\n- **DSL Entry Point**: `KStreamImpl.map()` (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamImpl.java:283-300)\\n- **Processor Implementation**: `KStreamMap.java` implements `ProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KOut, VOut>`\\n- **Inner Processor**: `KStreamMapProcessor extends ContextualProcessor<KIn, VIn, KOut, VOut>`\\n- **Key Pattern**: Transforms both key and value, changing key type (key-changing operation)\\n- **Record Flow**: `KeyValueMapper` applies transformation, `context().forward()` sends modified record\\n\\n**2. Filter Operation**\\n- **DSL Entry Point**: `KStreamImpl.filter()` (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamImpl.java:146-172)\\n- **Processor Implementation**: `KStreamFilter.java` implements `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<K, V, V>`\\n- **Inner Processor**: `KStreamFilterProcessor extends ContextualFixedKeyProcessor<K, V, V>`\\n- **Key Pattern**: Keeps fixed key, filters based on `Predicate<K, V>` test result\\n- **Record Flow**: Conditional forwarding using `context().forward(record)` only if predicate passes\\n\\n**3. MapValues Operation**\\n- **DSL Entry Point**: `KStreamImpl.mapValues()` (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamImpl.java:241-280)\\n- **Processor Implementation**: `KStreamMapValues.java` implements `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, VOut>`\\n- **Inner Processor**: `KStreamMapProcessor extends ContextualFixedKeyProcessor<KIn, VIn, VOut>`\\n- **Key Pattern**: Transforms value only, preserves key type\\n- **Record Flow**: `ValueMapperWithKey` transforms values, `context().forward()` sends modified record\\n\\n**4. GroupBy Operation**\\n- **DSL Entry Point**: `KStreamImpl.groupBy()` (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamImpl.java:693-716)\\n- **Repartitioning**: Creates a key-changing operation using `internalSelectKey()` which applies `KStreamMap`\\n- **Result**: Returns `KGroupedStreamImpl<KOut, V>` for downstream aggregations\\n- **GroupedStreamAggregateBuilder**: Orchestrates repartitioning and stateful aggregation processors\\n\\n### Extended DSL Operations\\n\\n**FlatMap/FlatMapValues**:\\n- `KStreamFlatMap.java`: Implements `ProcessorSupplier` for 1-to-many key-value transformations\\n- `KStreamFlatMapValues.java`: Implements `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier` for value-only expansions\\n\\n**Stateless Operations**:\\n- `KStreamPeek.java`: Implements `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier` for side-effects without modifying records\\n- `KStreamBranch.java`: Implements `ProcessorSupplier` for conditional routing to multiple child nodes\\n- `KStreamPrint.java`: Implements `ProcessorSupplier` for debugging/printing records\\n- `ForeachProcessor.java`: Implements `Processor` for terminal side-effect operations\\n\\n**Stateful Aggregation**:\\n- `KStreamReduce.java`: Implements `KStreamAggProcessorSupplier` for reduce operations with state stores\\n- `KStreamAggregate.java`: Implements `KStreamAggProcessorSupplier` for aggregate operations with initialization\\n- `KStreamWindowAggregate.java`: Time-windowed aggregation processor\\n- `KStreamSessionWindowAggregate.java`: Session-windowed aggregation processor\\n- `KStreamSlidingWindowAggregate.java`: Sliding window aggregation processor\\n\\n### KTable DSL Operations\\n\\n**KTable.filter()**:\\n- **Processor Implementation**: `KTableFilter.java` implements `KTableProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KIn, VIn>`\\n- **Inner Processor**: `KTableFilterProcessor implements Processor<KIn, Change<VIn>, KIn, Change<VIn>>`\\n- **State Management**: Materializes state store if queryable, tracks old/new values for changelog semantics\\n\\n**KTable.mapValues()**:\\n- **Processor Implementation**: `KTableMapValues.java` implements `KTableProcessorSupplier<KIn, VIn, KIn, VOut>`\\n- **Inner Processor**: `KTableMapValuesProcessor implements Processor<KIn, Change<VIn>, KIn, Change<VOut>>`\\n- **Change Records**: Operates on `Change<V>` wrappers to track old and new values for updates\\n\\n**KTable Joins**:\\n- `KTableKTableAbstractJoin.java`: Base for table-table joins (inner, left, right, outer)\\n- `KTableKTableInnerJoin.java`, `KTableKTableLeftJoin.java`, `KTableKTableRightJoin.java`, `KTableKTableOuterJoin.java`\\n- `KTableKTableJoinMerger.java`: Merges results from multiple join sides\\n\\n**KStream-KTable Joins**:\\n- `KStreamKTableJoin.java`: Stream-table join processor\\n- `KStreamKStreamJoin.java` and variants: Stream-stream joins with windowing\\n\\n### Implementation Patterns\\n\\n**KStream Pattern** (Key or Value Changing):\\n1. Call DSL method on `KStreamImpl` (e.g., `filter()`, `map()`)\\n2. Create `ProcessorParameters` with a `ProcessorSupplier` instance (e.g., `new KStreamFilter(predicate, false)`)\\n3. Wrap in `ProcessorGraphNode` for topology building\\n4. Return new `KStreamImpl` with graph node reference\\n5. Inner processor class extends `ContextualProcessor` or `ContextualFixedKeyProcessor`\\n6. Process method calls `context().forward()` to send records downstream\\n\\n**KTable Pattern** (Stateful):\\n1. Call DSL method on `KTableImpl` (e.g., `filter()`, `mapValues()`)\\n2. Create processor supplier implementing `KTableProcessorSupplier`\\n3. Processor receives/sends `Change<V>` records (tracking old and new values)\\n4. Materializes state store for queryability and changelog management\\n5. Manages old value state for changelog semantics\\n\\n**Grouping Pattern**:\\n1. `KStreamImpl.groupBy()` creates key selection using `internalSelectKey()` \\n2. Returns `KGroupedStreamImpl` which chains to aggregation builders\\n3. `GroupedStreamAggregateBuilder` orchestrates repartitioning and aggregation processor deployment\\n4. Aggregation processors use state stores for incremental computations\\n\\n### Migration Implications\\n\\nFor teams migrating from DSL to Processor API for custom state store management:\\n\\n1. **Direct Replacement**: Single-operation transformations (map, filter, mapValues) can be replaced with corresponding `Processor` implementations\\n\\n2. **State Store Access**: KTable and aggregation operations require understanding of `Change<V>` records and state store lifecycle (`init()`, `close()` methods)\\n\\n3. **Record Forwarding**: DSL `context().forward()` calls must be preserved in custom processors for proper topology connectivity\\n\\n4. **Processor Suppliers**: Must implement appropriate supplier interfaces (`ProcessorSupplier`, `FixedKeyProcessorSupplier`, `KTableProcessorSupplier`)\\n\\n5. **State Management**: Stateful operations require explicit `StoreBuilder` configuration and `StoreFactory` integration\\n\\nThe clear separation between `FixedKeyProcessor` (for same-key transformations) and `Processor` (for key-changing transformations) enables compiler-level safety and performance optimizations by avoiding unnecessary key serialization overhead.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
